Pomfrey were simply set aside.On the third night of his bed rest, Severus came to Harry's room, as always. Harry was lying on his bed, eyes closed. Severus knocked on the door lightly, peeking his head into the room. "Are you asleep?""Not quite," Harry answered, opening his eyes and stretching. Severus came into the room, grabbed the chair by the desk that sat in his room, and sat down on it."Then why were you lying down with your eyes closed?" Severus said conversationally, setting a couple of vials on his bed."I don't know. Just thinking, I guess," Harry said softly, watching Severus. Severus dismissed Harry's comment for the moment. He could tell Harry's voice was quite raspy, and he put his hand on Harry's forehead. "Still quite hot" Severus said, more to himself, getting out his wand and performing a spell to check Harry's vitals."You're not used to having to take care of someone sick, are you Severus?" Harry chuckled a bit."I've brewed quite a few spells over my time as Potions Master to deal with many different illnesses in fact, and I have assisted Mme. Pomfrey a few times when there have been an over-capacity of students in the hospital wing," Severus replied. "But taking care of someone specifically with an illnessno, I believe you are the first." Severus gave Harry a small smile. Severus placed all the vials on Harry's bedside table, and sat back as Harry sighed and downed the regular vials he had been required to drink for the past few days.Harry noticed a different, larger vial sitting there. "What's this?" Harry asked quizzically."Well  me and Mme. Pomfrey have been working on a little project.this illness of yours seems to be persisting a little more than either of us would like. So we've concocted a potion that we feel might just help the problem."Harry looked inquisitively at the vial, picking it up and surveying it."you're sure I'm not going to sprout antlers or anything, right?"Severus gave Harry an exasperated look, and Harry laughed. "Alright, alright." He put the vial to his mouth and drank it down in one shot. He choked slightly, causing him to cough and sputter slightly."Tastes horrid," Harry said as soon as he regained himself.Severus smirked. "Sorry, did I not warn you?"Harry shook his head, He put the vial down, about to lie down in his bed, when Severus held his shoulder and said, "Before you go to bed, can we try an exercise?"Harry raised an eyebrow."Humour me," Severus said.Harry sighed, slowly positioning himself back into a sitting position."Harry, forgive me for this, but I want you to try this Occlumency exercise. I know you're tired, but this gives you a chance to test out your own strength, as you might not always be in the best of mindsets when you need to block your mind."Harry nodded quietly, waiting for Severus to continue."Close your eyes." Harry did as he was told. "Remember what you have learned so far?"Harry nodded. Severus had told him that in the future, when he had built his mental shield stronger, he would have to work on channeling other, less threatening thoughts in his mind, in order to not reveal that he was actually performing Occlumency. But for now, he had to imagine himself in a scenario in which there was a state of peace. One where he could control his own thoughts. He envisioned himself on a broom: he was free-falling, looping throughout the fresh air, the sun shining brightly on him. He took a deep breath."Do you have a vision in your head?" Severus said quietly. Harry nodded."Okay, now, I want you to open your eyes, without losing the vision." Harry opened his eyes, keeping the image in his head. Admittedly, it was a lot harder, with all the visions of his surroundings."When you are performing Occlumency," Severus said, "you will more than likely not have your eyes closed. You will have to have your eyes open, and be communicating. For the past while, we have been working with trying to strengthen your control and your own mental shield. Now, we will not have you try to communicate just yet." Severus shifted, so that he was facing Harry directly, looking straight into his eyes. "I want you to just stare at me right now. Just look directly at me. Try to block me out, while you have the distractions of the surrounding area weakening the vision in your mind. Can you do that?" Harry nodded."Okay." Severus breathed, looked directly into Harry's eyes, and whispered, Legilimens.He could see the vision in Harry's mind. Flying. He should have figured. He could feel that it was weaker though. He had expected that. Not only was Harry slightly tired, but the distractions of the room certainly derailed his focus. He slowly prodded deeper, and he could feel the shield weakening and weakening. He was not planning to break the shield, but he did go a little deeper, trying to see how long Harry could hold his control,Suddenly, without expecting it, he felt the shield break.The image of the blue sky disappeared, and Severus was swept into a memory of Harry's. He could see a smaller version of Harryhe couldn't have been older than 6. He was running, a look a fear in his eyes. He was looking for a place to hide, but the house was not very big in itself. He tried to run upstairs, but suddenly, two boys came running from the corner and grabbed him, making Harry trip backwards down the first few stairs he had climbed."Think you can steal our candy, from us, eh?" One of the boys sneered as his friend had Harry by the scruff of his neck."DudleyI'm sorry, I just, wanted to try for once""Well, I'm so sorry mum didn't give you anybeen a naughty boy, probably. It's what mummy always says. Naughty boy, that Potter!"This "Dudley" kid.he looked about the same age! His friend about a year older.Young Harry started pulling at the hand around his collar. "Letmego!""Suit yourself, Potter!" Dudley nodded, and the other kid threw Harry into the wall. He hit the wall with a sound that made even Severus flinch. Harry remained crouched on the ground, holding is hand to his head, his arm slightly bleeding."And remember that next time you try to steal something from me!" he said, walking off with a smirk on his face, him and his friend laughing behind me, leaving Harry sitting on the ground.Severus was, just as suddenly, swept out of the memory, back in his own home. His face still carried a slightly startled expression. Harry sat on his bed, breathing heavily, looking down."Harry," Severus struggled to speak. "I'm sorry, I didn't mean  ""It's okay," Harry said quietly, still looking down. "My barrier was too weak. I know I need to get stronger."They both sat in silence. For once, Severus was truly at a loss for words. But it was Harry who broke the silence."My cousinhe never treated me well," Harry said quietly. "I mean, we lived pretty much in the same house, like brothers, and what brothers don't fight?" Harry paused for a moment. "But, you knowit's not like Ron with Fred and George, where they fight, but they always make up, and the truly care for eachother. You know, he never liked me. Neither did Uncle Vernonn or Aunt Petunia." His voice choked. "Didn't do a damn thing wrong. Always played by their rules. Butit wasn't enough. There was no changing what they thought about me. To them, I was this weird, insufferable freak." Harry breathed a hard sigh. His voice wavered as he tried to continue speaking. "It's likeit's like I never belonged anywhere."Severus, struggling, put a hand on his shoulder. "You're right Harry. You don't belong in that horrible, muggle house. You don't belong with those Dursleys, not a bit. You belong here." Severus stopped as he said this. "I mean.in the world you are now. With your friends, with Hogwarts. Here." Severus took his hand off Harry."You must be tired. If you want to speak with me in the morning, I'll be more than free to." Severus turned off Harry's lamp, and moved the back to the table, as Harry settled into bed. Before walking out the door, he said softly, "Goodnight." He met no response in turn as he walked out of the room.The truth was, he wouldn't have been able to stay in that room much longer. Anger bubbled inside him. These insufferable muggles, Lily's own SISTERhow could they have done this?! He knew Petunia had been much of a brat in their younger days, but to go this far? He went into the living room to sit down, but the tears began to fall down his eyes before he even reached his favourite seat. The flashbacks of his childhood spun around in his head. The pain, the struggle, not being accepted by his fatherhe had never felt like he had belonged! And look at where it has lead him! To choose the death-eaters, somewhere where he had thought he belonged. Choosing the darkness, the secrecy, the danger, the hurt. And realizing all too late, how much of a wrong choice he had made. He was abandoned: a spy, still living in the darkness. He was a misfit himself.He couldn't imagine Harry following the same path that he did.In anger, he quickly apparated out of the house. He reappeared in the hallowed streets of Godric's Hallow, right in front of Dumbledore's house. He was considering storming into the house without warning, but before he had even reached the door, it swung wide open, revealing Dumbledore in a light red nightgown, with gold linings."Severus. What brings you here this fine night?""I am not in the mood, Albus," Severus said sternly."Well, come in then." Dumbledore held the door open for him as Severus walked in with hard steps.Severus didn't even wait for Dumbledore to say anything. He turned right around on him, as Dumbledore had closed the door, and said in a stern tone, "How could you have let Harry suffer with so much all his life with his horrible uncle and aunt?"Severus, as soon as the words left his mouth, saw Dumbledore's face suddenly grew sad. Dumbledore put a sad smile on his face. "You knew that he hadn't lived a very good life," he said calmly."Yes, but I didn't expect that he had been treated like a slave!" Severus burst out, startling even Dumbledore. "The boy didn't have a friend in the world! In the month and a half that I have been with him, I have discovered more than you have cared to admit to me for 15 years!"Dumbledore, for once, did not have any words to say. He was silent for a moment, slowly going to his couch, and sitting down. He breathed a sigh, looking up at Severus. "It was the only place that was safe for him Severus.""Sure, that's what you say. That's what you've been saying all the time. Well, enlighten me," Severus' breath started to take a breathy tone. "How can a place where he is abused be safe for him? What kind of protection have these muggles given him that any wizard could not have provided for him? What kind of life do you expect him to live after everything that he has been through?!""Severus, you need to calm down," Dumbledore said, a slightly stern tone entering his own voice."I don't think I have to do anything, Albus," Severus said, his anger growing even stronger. "Did you even care about him? Were you really protecting him?""What about you, Severus?" Dumbledore answered. "Are you not just protecting him for Lily?"Severus stopped for a second. He looked Dumbledore straight in his eyes."I'm not just protecting him for Lily anymore."

AN: Hello all! For once, I was able to make this chapter in a month and a week. Hoping you guys enjoy the chapter, and as always, leave me reviews, I love them :DChapter 25: A Trail of Broken GlassIt was half an hour later. Severus was sitting down, a glass of Scotch in his hand, Dumbledore across from him, a cup of tea in his down. Severus' head was bent down, staring into his glass."I'm truly sorry, Severus," Dumbledore replied. "That was inconsiderate of me to say.""And it was completely fair as well," Severus said, still staring into his glass. "This whole time, for 16 years, I had been protecting him only for Lily.although it's ironic to know that I never really had protected him after all.""Ofcourse you did Severus," Dumbledore said, leaning towards him. "You have saved his life many times over his past years at Hogwarts.""Perhaps. But how have I treated him?" Severus said slowly.Dumbledore was silent for a moment, staring into the soft fire crackling in the fireplace."And you seeevery year, he went back to that bloody placehe didn't even have a safe haven anywhere." Severus sighed. "I had always made his life a struggle, during the past five years."Dumbledore spoke slowly. "And why is that?""Well" Severus' voice got caught in his throat for a moment. "every time I looked at himhe reminded me of James."Dumbledore placed his tea cup on the table, and leant over to put his hand on Severus', who was starting to grasp his glass very tightly. "I hope you're starting to realize now thathe's not. He may be James' childbut he's not James."Severus sighed, his breath wavering. "I know that. I know. You just don't understand how hard that wasto see"Dumbledore had a sympathetic look on his face. "My boy, I understand. Views don't change very quickly." Dumbledore put his cup down on the table. "However, I would have to say...I believe yours have changed, have they?"Severus took another sip of his drink, the warm, alcoholic liquid running down his throat. He wasn't sure if the alcohol was calming him or making him more nervous, but due to his shaky breath, he figured the latter."Well, I am accustomed to barging into your house concerning insolent little students, aren't I?" Severus said sarcastically.Dumbledore smiled softly. "Remember, Severus  inside you, you have goodness. You may have been a death eater before, but that does not define you now. Trust me, my boy, when I say that you are not like them."Severus sighed, not being able to reply. He put his own glass on the table sharply, the liquid swishing, a drop landing on the table. He closed his eyes sharply, and when he opened them again, he was looking straight at Dumbledore."Just tell me one thing, Albus. And please tell me the truth." Severus was looking intently at him. "Do you actually care about Harry? Did you ever really care for him?"Dumbledore looked at Severus, a blank look on his face. He turned his gaze towards the cup, silent for a moment. Then, looking back at Severus, he replied, "Yes, I do care for Harry. I always have, since I left him on Petunia's doorstep. You don't know how much it pains me to put him through all this." He drifted off, looking at his cup again."I feel there is a 'but' in here somewhere," Severus said in a leveled tone, still looking at Dumbledore.Dumbledore sighed, closing his eyes. "He is our best hope. He is our only hope, Severus. You understand that."Severus' expression grew hard, an intense look on his face, when suddenly, he collapsed back into the couch, defeat registering inside him. He grabbed his glass and took a huge gulp."Well, he doesn't have to go this road alone," Severus said, looking down at the floor.Dumbledore smiled a genuine smile. "I wouldn't expect anything less, Severus."Harry rose in the morning, a sleepy yawn escaping from his lips. He sat up in his bed and stretched, feeling quite relaxed. He removed the covers from over him, and dragged his feet off the bed, stretching his legs and wiggling his toes. He stood up and went to the window, pulled away the curtains, and opened the window, feeling the light breeze come in. He closed his eyes and breathed in the fresh air. He was really starting to like this place. However, he just remembered, he had only about a week and a half left of the summer. He sighed as that realization came to him. He always loved to go back to Hogwarts. However this timesomething was different.He shrugged the feeling off, rubbing his eyes and walking towards the door, feeling the hunger in the pit of his stomach.Another realization came to him as soon as he thought of that  he felt hungry. He hadn't felt hungry since he had gotten the illness. And he had breathed in that fresh air properly.He swallowed. Slightly scratchy, still, but the pain of his sore throat had most of all disappeared. Other than his head feeling slightly fuzzy, it felt almost like a miracle. He walked out of the hallway, and as he entered the kitchen, he heard the sizzling of bacon and eggs. And he could also smell them!"Hello sleepyhead," Severus said. "Decided to sleep in today?""Hey, it's only.10:30 AM." Harry claimed, yawning."You're going back to Hogwarts in less than two weeks," Severus said, taking the eggs and bacon off of the frying pan and placing them on to a plate. He turned around to the dining table, where Harry had already seated himself, and put the plate on the table, Harry's mouth watering at the delicious smell. "I think I should start waking you up at 7 AM, get you back on a regular sleeping schedule."Harry groaned, as Severus chuckled. "Now why don't you get up and make yourself useful, and get some plates and utensils?"Harry shook his head, but he was smiling. It was a comfortable morning routine. And he liked it. A feeling of emptiness nagged at him slightly, but he shook it off again as he rose out of the chair to help set the table.They were about halfway through breakfast. Harry was hoarding the bacon, drinking a cup of coffee, while Severus was calmly taking a sip of his own tea. He shook his head, watching Harry eat, but he dismissed it because Harry had not been eating much all week."So what have you got planned for today?" Harry asked, mouth full of bacon."I'm not sure I understood you with your mouth full," Severus said reproachfully."Sorry," Harry apologized, swallowing his food with a guilty look on his face.Severus smiled. "I have to start getting things ready for the new school year. And you," Harry rose his eyebrows as Severus looked straight at him, "Are going shopping for new school attire and materials.""Really?" Harry said in surprise, putting his cup of coffee down. "Who is going to take me then?""Professor McGonagall will escort you to Diagon Alley to purchase some new robes for you, and to get you your new textbooks and supplies. I dare say your robes are getting quite short for your height. When was the last time you had new ones made for you?"Harry shrugged. "Before third year, I think? I don't remember too well. It has been awhile. The last time, Mrs. Weasley made sure I had gotten new ones, but since then, everything's been a little hectic."Severus' heart ached silently for the boy who didn't even have anyone to take him to get proper school robes when needed."Well, we will definitely make sure you have everything you will need, and that everything will fit properly too," Severus said. "Perhaps you might even meet Mr. Weasley and Mrs. Granger as well. How does that sound?""It sounds great," Harry smiled. "It'll be nice to get outand also nice to see Minerva again."Severus raised his eyebrows.Harry put his hands up, a cheeky grin on his face, "She said I can call her that."Severus shook his head, although chuckling slightly to himself. "Try to refer to her as Mrs. McGonagall during school hours, alright?""Okay," Harry said, taking his fork to get another scoop of bacon. He stopped suddenly as a thought came to him. "Wait, hold onyou had to have had this all planned out earlier, right?" Severus nodded. "But I was just about confined to my bed right up until last night! So how did you?"Severus smirked. "Confidence in my potion-creating techniques?"Harry gave Severus a little jab across the table, and both of them laughed. But Severus could see Harry's silent thank you."And hey, since you seem to be feeling quite better now, I think, after you get back, is a great time to get started on the rest of your summer homework, young man."Harry groaned again, and Severus laughed.I promise you. You won't have to go through this road alone.Harry was in his room changing when Minerva arrived."So, Severus, potion worked, as you expected?" Minerva said, smiling as she arrived through the floo."Am I ever wrong about these things, Minerva?" Severus joked.Minerva gave him a reproachful look.Severus chuckled. "Well, his symptoms are not entirely gone, still a bit of a scratchy throat and some dizziness, I've given him another dose right after breakfast. If he seems to feel faint or anything ""Don't worry, I'll let you know," Minerva said. "He's in safe hands.""You know, you're perhaps one of the only people I can trust saying those words," Severus commented."Well I'm honoured," Minerva smiled. "Have you ever gotten down to the root of this situation?""It's complicated," Severus shook his head. "Whatever it is, it is no good for us. At all.""Just relax, Severus," Minerva said calmly. "We don't really know anything yet.""We know that Draco Malfoy attacked Harry and Lupin with an intent to do some good damage.""We don't know what happened there, Severus," Minerva said, but from the look on Severus' face, she could tell that he was thinking that she couldn't even deny it."You two had better be off," Severus said. "I'll get the pack rat right now." Minerva chuckled as Severus walked towards the bedroom hallway.He knocked on the door of Harry's room. He could hear a low mumble on the other side. "Don't make me drag you out of there, Harry." Just as soon as the words had left his mouth, Harry walked out, a smile on his face. He was wearing a white-collared shirt over a solid red shirt, with a new pair of jeans. He shook his head in dismay as he saw the turned up collar."If you want to be a gentleman, you might as well atleast dress the part," Severus said, turning down his collar as Harry rolled his eyes. Severus leaned down towards Harry. "Now I want you to remember, stay with Minerva, don't waste time, get everything you need, and  "" don't do anything foolish," Harry finished. Severus looked at him, a face he hadn't really looked at for 5 years, and smiled."And stay safe," Severus said. "Can you promise me that?""Yes," Harry said, smiling back.When Harry apparated away with Minerva, Severus wasn't so sure.There were few days when the Malfoy Manor was rid of the wards of Death Eaters that felt like they had the entitlement to be there whenever they wanted to. But then again, with the way things were, I guess they did now. Atleast, under the Dark Lord's orders.But today, it was empty. Lucius stood in front of a large window, watching the sky grow darker. His hands were crossed around his chest, and he had a vacant look on his face, as he stared out into the setting sun.He felt a hand lay softly on his shoulder. "Lucius."He didn't answer, but the voice of Narcissa made him feel slightly calmer."What's wrong?" Narcissa said, in a soothing voice, putting her other hand on his other shoulder.Lucius still couldn't speak. More so, he couldn't put his thoughts into words."All of themAlecto, Amycus, Dolohov, Goyle, Yaxley.thinking they can come and just walk around the manor like they own it," were the first words to come out of his mouth.Narcissa started to massage his shoulders, but it didn't help. He walked away from Narcissa, pacing away from the window."I know it's a bit of a mess around here" Narcissa said softly."Around here? This whole thing is a mess!" Lucius hissed, causing Narcissa to draw back slightly.He noticed her action, and he walked back to her, taking her two hands in his. "It shouldn't be this way. It wasn't this way. We were not made the scum of the earth. If it wasn't for the stupid Potter boy, none of this would be happening."Narcissa didn't speak, but just held his hands, looking at him, a silent comfort."Now, that damned Severus Snape is at the Dark Lord's right hand, while we are barely escaping death at this moment.""Now don't say that," Narcissa said, putting a hand up to his face."It's true." Lucius' voice was drawing to a hiss once again. "Since the Department of Mysteries fiasco" Lucius couldn't find the words to say, anger heating up inside of him. "I don't know what's going on with Severus and the Potter boy.""Whatever it was, I'm sure it was under Dumbledore's orders. You know the position he's in.""I know that, Narcissa," Lucius said, frustrated. "However, I also know that the Dark Lord is unaware of this little situation. As the Dark Lord's main man, I believe this is something that would be very important to mention""Lucius"A shadowed look came across Lucius' face. "What is he? A mere half blood who was lucky to get on his good side. I've been serving the Dark all this time! And up until now, I WAS his main man!"Lucius was starting to become even angrier. "That Potter boy has caused too many problems, and now I find him and Severus together in Paris? And the way that Severus immediately found the boy and took him awaymaybe Bellatrix was right in not trusting him." Lucius mused. "I think it's about time that the Dark Lord knew what was going on around here.""Lucius, no." Narcissa said sharply as soon as Lucius had finished speaking.Lucius gave her a dark look. "What?""Lucius, listen to me," Narcissa said urgently. "We don't know what's happening. And right now, we can't afford any mistakes." Narcissa voice was steady, staring straight into Lucius' eyes. "And he is the only one at Hogwarts who can protect Draco.""I thought he made an unbreakable vow?" Lucius said, still in anger."An unbreakable vow is hard to keep if there are no means to. If he falls in the Dark Lord's eyes, and is sent away from Hogwarts, then he cannot protect him. Your son will be on his own."Lucius didn't speak, her words resonating in his head. He was furious. Furious that Harry Potter had him defeated and sent to Azkaban, causing him to fail his mission. Furious that Severus was now practically the Dark Lord's second in command, while the Malfoys were the laughing stock of the Death Eater crowd. Furious that his and his family's life was starting to come into shambles.But he sighed in defeat. Narcissa was right. It was like a trail of broken glass. Every piece connected, in some weird, absurd way.The two stared at eachother, hands held in eachother's, as the last of the sun's light set over the horizon.

If you are new, please let me know as well! I'd love to know that people will still continue to read this, and what you guys are thinking and looking forward to. I hope I have not lost my touch. Love you all, and keep tuned for more!Chapter 26: A Piece of FamiliarityThey had apparated in a dark corner right outside the Leaky Cauldron, Minerva still grasping Harry's hand. Minerva said, looking concerned at Harry."Mmm, never better." Harry said, as he regained his balance."Do you have your list of school supplies?"Harry held up a piece of parchment with Minerva's own unique scrawl, and she smiled."Very good. Let's get on it, then, we have a lot to purchase." Minerva looked around very discreetly, and, still holding Harry hand, guided him quickly inside the bar.As they opened the door, the familiar ring of the bell at the front of the Leaky Cauldron rang. Harry looked around, the familiar image of wizards and witches alike, some along the bar table on the uncomfortable stools, some lounging around the rest of the bar, the smell of drinks he could not distinguish.it was nice to be somewhere familiar for once. He had felt like his life seemed much less than familiar these days."Hello, Harry!" Harry turned around to the bright, recognizable face of Hagrid, his first ever real friend. His face brightened immediately. He hadn't seen him all summer."Hi Hagrid! How you been?""Ahh, well, been crazy all o'er London, gotta tell yeh. Been working with Dumbledore, doin' this and that. How abou' yeh? Heard you bin stayin' with mean old Snape, have yeh?"Harry smiled. "He's not so bad.""I know, Harry, I know. Jus' pullin' yer leg. Real nice for him to take yeh in." Hagrid leaned down on his knee towards Harry, although even then, he was still a few heads taller than him."Real sorry 'bout Sirius, Harry. He was a good man, knew him mos' of me life. Fought his life fer ev'ryone he cared 'bout. And he cared 'bout yeh."Harry nodded, a solemn look on his face."Come on, Harry, we must get going," Minerva said, a hand on Harry's shoulder, giving Hagrid a very stern look. Hagrid slightly shrugged, stood up, and gave Harry a pat on the back that almost threw him off his feet. "I'll meet yeh la'er in Diagon Alley, Harry, I still got ter still give yeh yer birthday present!"Harry laughed. "Thanks Hagrid, I'll definitely see you later on."Harry waved, as Minerva took his hand and rushed him ahead, Hagrid looking back with a nostalgic look in his eyes.As they reached the back door and stepped outside, Minerva looked over towards Harry and saw a distant look on his face."Now Harry, don't be so down. I think I know what will help you feel better."Harry raised an eyebrow, but did not reply. He watched as Minerva tapped, with her wand, the secret pattern that he had seen Hagrid do all those years ago, which opened a secret wall, into what everyone knew as in the infamous Diagon Alley.Harry's eyes brightened slightly as he looked at the place where he was first introduced to the wizarding world  where he had bought his first wand, where he had gotten Hedwig, where he had roamed during those few weeks before third year when he had ran away from the Dursleysas many times as he was there, he never got over seeing the pure magic of the place, especially after two months of being stuck with the Dursleys.Minerva smiled as she saw Harry's widened eyes. "Come, Harry, we have a lot to shop for." Harry followed her, glancing around at all the shops with bright eyes. They passed Flourish and Blotts, Eeylops Owl Emporium, Magical Menagerie, Quality Quidditch Supplies (Minerva had to slightly drag him as he had his eye on these fancy Quidditch gloves being displayed inside the main window)"Minerva," Harry said, as they hustled through the many parents and children, some licking colourful lollypops from Sugarplum's Sweets Shop, some playing with new broomsticks, and more, "where are we going? We're passing all the shops where we need to go!""Just a moment, Mr. Potter," Minerva said with a little smirk. "There is one little stop we must make first."They walked for another minute longer, until they had reached Florean Fortescue's Ice Cream Parlour. As they walked up towards, Harry caught a glint of red hair. He also heard a familiar voice  "Come on Fred, you have your own ice cream! Get off of mine!""Ron!" Harry shouted happily, and Ron turned his head around."Harry!" he shouted in return, his mouth full of ice cream.Ron passed his ice cream over to George, and the two best friends ran up towards each other, into something like a big bear hug. They heard one of the Weasley twins whistle behind them, and Ron let go of the embrace, shouting an irritated "Shut it, George!", shaking his head. "I've missed ya, mate.""Same," Harry said, a big smile on his face. "You owe me a game of Quidditch, you know.""I don't know, do you really think you're a match for me?" Ron joked."I don't think you'd be a match for the broom on its own, Ron," Fred said, both him and George popping out from behind Ron the both of them laughing. Ron grabbed his ice cream from George and scowled, Harry laughing in spite of himself."How ya been, Harry ol' pal?" George chimed in."Alright, I guess," Harry said half-heartedly."Well you know what you've been missing, right?" Fred said."A good old time with us, that's what!" George jumped in, patting Harry's back. "And mate, have we got something to show you!" He winked."Harry," Minerva interrupted the boys' banter. "How about you go grab yourself an ice cream, and maybe we can all go and get your school supplies for the year." She placed a few coins in his hand, urging him ahead. Harry ran with the three boys towards the door of the shop, while Minerva sighed and shook her head amusedly.Once they got to the door, they stopped as they saw it open. Hermoine and Ginny both walked out, each licking a cone of colourful ice cream. Hermione looked up, and when she saw Harry there, she ran up to him, ice cream in hand, and jumped to give him a hug as well. "Harry!""Woah," Harry exclaimed, thrown off his balance for the third time today. "Hey, Hermione!""How've you been?" Hermione said brightly. Ginny stood to the side, a content look on her face, engrossed in her icecream, and Harry couldn't help stealing a sidelong glance at her before returning his gaze to Hermione. "Well I mean, after I've finally been cured fromwhatever illness I had, definitely better." Harry looked away, but Hermione gave him a sympathetic look. Of course Hermione knew. Knew about the unknown spell that had him bedridden for almost a week. Ron had to know too. The twins as well, and Ginny. Things never really stayed a secret for long between the Order, especially when it concerned him.Suddenly, Harry felt very vulnerable. It seemed like he was always the one getting into situations like these, and it was always him that those sympathetic looks were thrown at. One mere spell had him knocked out for a week! He had seen enough sympathetic looks before the summer had started. Although Dumbledore had helped him, and had tried to keep too many people away from him during the time, he still saw it  the faces of sympathy and pity on all the student's faces, even the ones not in Gryffindor.Ron noticed an absent look in Harry's eyes, and he ran up to his first best friend, putting an arm around his shoulder. "Of course you're better, mate. You're here now. This ice cream, mate, you know, if I could, I would marry ice cream""Well I'm sure you'll get sick of it once your teeth start to rot," Mrs. Weasley walked out the door, Mr. Weasley following right behind. Ron looked at Harry and rolled his eyes, causing Harry to snicker."Harry, my boy!" Mrs. Weasley said when she saw Harry, walking up to him and giving him a bear hug that only Mrs. Weasley could give. "We've all missed you so! How have you been? Taking care of yourself?" She leaned down, grabbed Harry's chin, and gave him a once over. "Severus has been feeding you right." She stood up, a big smile on her face. "Well then, let's get a move on, we don't have all day  Fred and George, cut it out!" She grabbed both of the boys' hands, as they protested, dragging them along. Ron and Hermione followed her, as did Ginny, but not without stopping beside Harry and giving him a little playful nudge. Harry looked ahead, to where she saw Mrs. Weasley greet Minerva.This was family. Lately, his family seemed to be growing.The teens walked along the streets of Diagon Alley, slowly licking on their ice cream cones (Mrs. Weasley had purchased a cone of cookie dough ice cream for Harry), catching up on the latest news.Ron told Harry all about the trip his family had taken to Paris ("They have a huge tower there, mate! You can see the whole world from the top  it's like flying without the possibility of dying!"). Harry chuckled to himself as Ron went on and on about their cuisine, like their butter croissants, this thing they called "poutine", which was a heavenly mixture of fries, gravy, and cheese. It gave Harry a nostalgic feeling as he remembered the time he and Severus went to France. Even since that short time ago, it feels like so much has changed.But as he watched Fred whack George on the head for trying to steal a lick of icecream, and as Hermione was talking to Ginny the courses she planned to take this year, he smiled as he remembered that much was still the same.After much jostling from Mrs. Weasley, everyone started shopping for their school materials. Minerva chuckled as Fred and George convinced Ron to open a book which caused a loud shriek to bellow throughout the store. Her eyes shifted over to Harry, who was quietly examining the books in the magical fiction section. Her eyes softened as she saw Harry's eyes light up as he pulled a book out the shelves. It seemed to be about witch folklore and myths. She chuckled.Minerva cared about all her students  she may be harsh sometimes, but she had a motherly inclination towards them, especially the ones in her house (although not quite as motherly as Mrs. Weasley). Perhaps it was from the fact that she had no real children of her own. But as she looked at Harry, she felt something stronger  she truly wanted to help, if in any way, ease the struggles of the Boy Who Lived. She felt a push inside her to be one of the protective figures Harry never had.Harry glanced over at Minerva, and, surprised to see her staring at him, gave an awkward smile. Minerva snapped out of her thoughts, and walked over to Harry, smirking, "I'm afraid witch folklore will not help you in your studies, Harry."Harry towards her with a smirk of his own. "You know, you've seemed to have acquired that signature smirk of Severus'.""Who says he didn't acquire it from me?" Minerva said, turning around and walking back towards the others, but turning around and giving a slight wink to Harry before continuing on.Harry shook his head, amused. Minerva and Severus. they were kind of alike, when he really thought about it. Their sarcasm was one to rival with.After a couple of hours, they had all finally gotten all the supplies that they needed. Hermione was admiring the new set of gold quills she purchased, while Harry had convinced Minerva to let him purchase those Quidditch gloves that Harry had been eyeing earlier (Minerva really did want Gryffindor to win the Quidditch cup this time around).As they were lugging their school supplies across the street, with Fred and George leading the pack, the two suddenly stopped in their tracks, causing Ginny to almost tumble over with her stuff. She scowled at them as Mrs. Weasley helped her straighten herself. "What's the hold up?!"Fred and George turned around towards Harry, a sly grin on their faces. "So remember when we told ya we had something to show ya?" George wrapped a hand around Harry's shoulder and guided him towards a peach-colored door to a building that, Harry realized, he didn't actually recognize. Fred stood behind Harry and covered his eyes before Harry could examine what the building was. "Guys!" Harry whined, but George put a finger to his lips."Can't ruin the surprise, Harry!" George said, as the two opened the door and guided Harry inside, very nearly slamming the door into Harry's side, if Hermione had not ran over to grab the door, with her own scowl on her face.Harry could hear people buzzing around him. There were sounds of laughter from children, chatter from people that sounded like they were about his age. Fred and George kept guiding until they finally settled in a spot that they deemed appropriate."Harrywelcome to Weasley's Wizard Wheezes!" they both exclaimed as Fred removed his hands from Harry's eyes.It was magnificent.All around him were moving knick knacks and things exploding, as children laughed at the different creations that lay around the store. He saw Extendable Ears, Skiving Snackboxes, and a piece of gum that turned the person who was chewing it completely blue. "Got it from a muggle movie dad brought home once," the twins had explained when Harry was staring at it.Harry was smiling from ear to ear. He could not believe what the twins had created, but he was quite happy for them. He remembered how he had given the twins the money they needed, from winning the Tri-wizard tournament, in order to open up a shop in the future."So what do ya think?" Fred asked Harry as George was speaking to some young girls about the assortment of love potions that were on display."It's brilliant," Harry smiled at him. "Really, guys, this is amazing."Fred and George returned a big smile. "Stay as long as you like, mate. We've got to get back to work, but we'll catch you after." They ran off after a child who was trying to sneak a pack of skiving snackboxes out of the store without paying.Harry turned to Ron with an incredulous look on his face."Wicked, isn't it?" Ron replied, grinning.Harry nodded. It was great to be back.After about a half hour marveling at the new joke shop, Mrs. Weasley and Minerva finally guided them out to finish buying the rest of their school supplies. Ron had failed in convincing Mrs. Weasley to buy them all more ice cream ("You'll spoil your dinner, Ron, really."). They were passing by Ollivander's, and Harry had a sudden inclination."Hey guys, you go on ahead and finish buying the last of your things. I want to pop into Ollivander's quickly."Ron and Hermione gave him a curious look, but shrugged as they waved goodbye to Harry and agreed to meet at Flourish and Blotts in 15 minutes. Harry walked over to the door, and slowly opened it. He heard a ring of bells as he almost tip-toed into the quiet store.It had that same magical energy that it did the first time he walked in here. A feeling of mystery, of power  of potential. In here were thousands of the very tools that tap into to a wizard's power  the power to perform magic.He had been there for not even 30 seconds when he heard a pair of wheels sliding, and there he was  the great Ollivander. He had not spoken to him since his first year, when he first bought his wand. When he had first begun to learn about his past."Well . if it isn't Harry Potter. Charmed to see you again.""Hello," Harry said. He suddenly felt as shy as he had that first year as well.Ollivander walked up to Harry slowly, almost examining him. "It looks like you have been doing great things, haven't you now."Harry chuckled as he remembered what Ollivander had told him during his first year. "Nothing that great, really.""Well, I'd say fighting off the Dark Lord 3 or 4 times qualifies as something great, wouldn't you think?"Harry gave a nervous breath. To think about that fact was a little hard for him to swallow, given everything that has happened to him so far. Harry pondered in front of Ollivander for a moment, something laying on the tip of his tongue."You have a question for me," Ollivander commented. It was not a question, but a statement.Harry looked up toward the old man. "Mr. Ollivanderwhat was it like when you first met You-Know-Who? When he first bought his wand?"Ollivander did not look disgusted or shocked by the question. He looked to one of the upper walls of wands, a blank look on his face  but there was a deepness in his eyes. "He was a quiet boy, that one. He was alone, not a parent or guardian with him. He came in with a certain air of  poise, you might call it. You could tell there was a determination in his eye  I had no doubt that he would end up in Slytherin house. Took me some time to find a wand that would choose him."He grew quiet for a second. "He asked me one question before he left my store.""What was it?" Harry asked, quietly watching his face.Ollivander paused for a moment. "He asked me, 'If you had all the power in the world, what would you do with it?'"Harry gulped slightly. "And what did you answer with?""I said to him, 'Power is a curious thing. Many wizards go to extreme lengths to gain a semblance of strength, certaintycontrol. But power comes at a price. It's about what price you're willing to pay for that power.'"Ollivander looked down at Harry, and with a calm look on his face, he said, "Good day to you, Harry Potter." He walked away, back to his shelves of wands, twiddling his thumbs in his pockets.Harry turned away towards the door, shaking his head slightly. What Ollivander had said rang in his head, though  what price was Tom Riddle ready to pay, at 11 years old?Harry opened the door, listening to the jingling of bells as it swung open. Harry bumped into something that was right in front of the door. As Harry looked at what he had ran into, he gulped harder as he saw a familiar cane, and the unmistakable long, blonde-white hair.

AN: I know, I know, it's been another 8 months. You're probably disappointed in me. I'm pretty disappointed in myself too. I'll be completely honest, over half of this chapter had been written months ago. The reason why it took so longfor me to finish the chapter and release it  I took quite a long time thinking about where I felt the story was going. It had (heart-breakingly) been years since I had touched this story, so it involved a lot of inserting myself back into the story,feeling out all the characters again, and thinking about where I wanted it to go. Considering even a sequel in the future (yes, I would still love to write a sequel, if you guys wanted it!). And I truly wanted to write when I had the time and themotivation too  and as a fourth year, entering fifth year, university student, those times don't come all that often. I am truly thankful for all those who continue to read  please continue to review, it's what keeps me wanting to write and wantingto release chapters sooner! I hope you can forgive me for the torturous long waits. In any case, enjoy the chapter!(On a side note, has anyone gotten and read Cursed Child? I got it at midnight release and AAAH I loved it so much!)Chapter 27: MissingHarry looked up into the face of none other than Lucius Malfoy.Lucius swore under his breath, and looked down to see what the cause of collision was. As soon as he saw Harry in front of him, his eyes narrowed. "Potter.""Lucius," answered Harry in return, in a guarded tone."What brings you to Diagon Alley all on your own?" Lucius said. Harry swear he could see the hint of a menacing smirk on his face. He was reminded all too well of the last run in he had had with this man  when Severus was forced to reveal that Harrywas 'temporarily' under his care."Shopping for school applies. Like all other Hogwarts students," he waved to the air around him in a sort of mocking gesture. Lucius scowled. Harry was not sure what was making him so fool-hardy with his words  but he had to almost stop himself fromsmirking. "I could ask you the same question.""If you must know, my wand seems to be a littlebent out of shape, so to speak. I'm here to get it mended." Lucius stated.Harry watched Lucius very closely. He was not sure how long this 'barely' civil conversation would last."It is quite peculiar to see you on your own, Mr. Potter. Surely your guardian could not see you to purchase your things?"Harry was about to retort, but he froze in his spot. Something did not feel right. He looked up at Lucius. He was looking calmly down at him, as if waiting for his question to be answered.But something wasn't right. Harry recognized this feeling. The feeling of someone trying to slip into the corners of his mind.It took him a few second to realize  Lucius was trying to perform Legilimency on him.Harry stared back at Lucius, pulling up the picture of his little meadow  the meadow he had first envisioned when Severus started teaching him Occlumency again this summer. It had been some time since Severus and Harry had had an Occlumency lesson, andHarry knew he was weaker. Lucius tried to slip through the folds of his meadow, quite shocked at first of the fact that Harry was actually trying to block out his spell. Harry started to struggle, which anyone could visibly see by the way he slightlyshook and how his eyes began squint, as the weight of the spell was beginning to break through his barrier. He finally closed his eyes, abandoning all pretenses of normal conversation  his only goal being trying to keep this bastard out of his mind.If Lucius could break through his barrier  there was no telling what danger everyone would be in.Minerva was walking back towards Ollivander's. Mr. Weasley and Ms. Granger had informed her about Harry's whereabouts, and they had begun to worry when Harry was 5 minutes late in meeting with them. What Minerva saw when she turned the corner made herfreeze in her steps.She was met with the view of Lucius Malfoy and Harry Potter standing facing eachother, in what almost looked like a stare-off. However, she could see Harry shaking, his eyes closed and his hands balled up into fists.Before any one of them could tell, Minerva was right by Harry's side, putting a hand on his shoulder. "What seems to be the problem here?" Lucius was shocked out of the spell, and Harry almost gasped at the release of weight from him. He opened his eyesand looked fearfully up at Minerva."No problem at allMinerva," Lucius said, a glare on his pale face. He nodded towards her, flirting a final smirk before he stalked passed the two, walking into Ollivander's.When Harry started to get a bearing on his surroundings again, he collapsed slightly into Minerva's arms, and she had to balance herself so that the both of them would not topple over. Blocking the spell had put a great mental strain on Harry's mind he had never experienced an attack like that before."Harry, what's wrong? What happened?" Minerva said, a concerned tone lacing her voice. All Harry could do was shake his head."Can you stand up straight?" Minerva asked. Harry took a deep breath and nodded. Minerva righted Harry, and he took another deep breath before he looked back up at Minerva, not knowing what his expression gave away."I think it's time that we take you back home, and maybe we can sit and talk about this with Severus, what do you say?" Minerva said, still looking at Harry with concern. She did not know what had happened, but whatever it was, she knew it was more thanHarry was letting on.Harry nodded half-heartedly. At this rate, he thought that Severus would never let him out of his house anymore.They walked back to the others, not speaking. Harry was still trying to recover from the last 5 minutes, and his mind was running in circles. Minerva did not interrupt his train of thought.He bid goodbye to Ron and Hermione, who were both disappointed that he could not stay longer, and also concerned over why Harry spoke not more than 10 words as he said his farewells. Minerva promised that they could get back together atleast once morebefore term started.She reached out towards Harry's hand, and bracing himself, he grabbed onto it, and they both disapparated away.Severus had been relaxing in his chair, reading a potions manual, when he heard a knock at his door. Severus raised an eyebrow, put the manual down, and walked towards the door. He peeked through the little peephole, and opened the door with a dubioussmirk. "The door, Minerva?""I figured it would be more appropriate, given the unexpected time of our arrival." Minerva answered, her voice sounding heavy. Severus took a look at the clock on the wall  it was 4:30 PM. She was right, he did not expect them home for a few more hours he had expected that Harry would have spent more time with his friends after they had purchased their things.He looked back to Minerva's face, and could see that it was etched with worry. Harry was very quiet, and upon looking at him, noticed that he looked very reserved.Severus braced himself for the worst."Come in," Severus said, as calmly as he could. Minerva and Harry both stepped in. Minerva subtly guided Harry towards the couch in the sitting room. They sat there quietly as Severus brought out two cups of tea, and one cup of coffee (Harry looked likedhe needed it). Harry muttered a quiet "Thank you" as Severus handed him his cup. Minerva took hers, added two sugars and one cream, and stirred it slowly  apparently not knowing how to start this conversation either."So. What happened?" Severus said. "I can see the somber looks on both of your faces, and that does not bode good news."Minerva stopped stirring, and put her cup down. "That would be a question for Harry."Severus raised an eyebrow, and turned to look at Harry. He had his head down, taking a tiny sip of his coffee. He avoided either of the two professors' gazes."Harry?" Severus said. Harry shook his head slightly, almost as if to himself."Harry, hey." Severus leaned over, placed his hand under Harry's chin, and lifted it up so he was looking in his eyes. The look of fear that Harry returned unnerved Severus. "It's okay. Whatever happened, you can tell us. You know we're here for you,right?"It took a few seconds, but Harry nodded. Severus leaned back, and took a sip of his tea. After another ten seconds, Harry finally spoke."I went to Ollivander's for a few minutes, telling Ron and Hermione that I'd meet them in 5 minutes. When I got outI ran into Lucius Malfoy." Harry took a deep breath, still looking down into his mug. "He tried to talk to me for about 30 seconds, askingme where my 'guardian' was." This is where Harry stopped. He looked up at Severus, and Severus gave him an encouraging nod."And then Lucius tried to use Legilimency on me."The look on both Severus' and Minerva's face could only be described as stunned. Severus tried to keep a straight face, but Minerva looked as if a tear might run down her face if she let it  which was a rare thing for Minerva."Tried?" Severus replied. "Did hesucceed?""No." Harry said, looking back into his mug. "I tried as hard as I could to block him out. Thankfully, Minerva came just in time, before it became to strong for me to keep out." Harry put down his mug, having only taken a couple of sips from it. "Is italright if I go to my room for a little bit? Please?""Alright." Severus answered. Harry got up, trying not to look the others in the eye, and walked out of the sitting room, towards his bedroom.As soon as he left, Minerva looked at Severus. "Severuswhat does this mean?""It meansthat Lucius is becoming suspicious." Severus sighed loudly, leaning back against the couch. On the outside, Severus seemed just agitated. On the inside however, Severus' mind was spinning with all the disastrous possibilities that could haveoccurred. What would have happened if Lucius had broken through Harry's barrier? What secrets would have escaped? How much danger would Harry's life have been in?"It also means our Occlumency lessons must go back in full swing." Severus shook his head. "Thanks for today, Minerva. You might as well go home and get some rest. I think we all need it."Minerva nodded. She finished her tea, got up, and before she got into the fireplace to floo away, she turned around towards him. "Severus  ""I'll talk to Harry," Severus nodded. Minerva nodded back, and she scooped up some floo powder, saying "Hogwarts"  and through the fire, she disappeared.Severus sighed, downing the rest of tea, craving something stronger. He stood up and slowly walked to Harry's room. Severus knocked softly twice, but no answer came from the room. He opened the door, and found Harry fast asleep. He had not changed  itlooked like he had crashed from exhaustion.Severus walked in quietly, careful not to wake Harry up, and pulled the covers up over his shoulders. He shook his head as he watched Harry sleep for a minute. Never would he have thought that Harry Potter would be sleeping in a bed in his home. If anyonehad told Severus that this is how his summer would turn out, he would have laughed in their face.Severus continued to look at Harry's face. There was something calm in that expression  the bliss that sleep brought on, he was sure, from the chaos that was the life of The Boy Who Lived.Severus realized that he had been watching Harry sleep for five minutes now. He tensed up, ignoring the paternal feeling he had briefly felt, and walked out of his room to clean up and retire to his room. That is, when the shock of his arm burning causedhim to drop both mugs in his hand. Cursing, he waved his wand, the broken pieces of glass vanishing from the floor.He quickly sent a patronus to Minerva: Minerva, I am being called. Contact Albus and Lupin for me. Have one of them come and watch Harry until I return. Minerva was prompt. Not 30 seconds later, as Severus had hastily put on the robes he reserved for such unpleasant occasions, he received Minerva's reply from her own Patronus:Albus is out of the castle attending to some Hogwarts matters. I sent a patronus to Remus, but there's no response. I will come myself and watch him.Severus did not have time to send a thank you patronus back, but truly he was thankful. He smiled a small smile to himself. It was good to know there was someone who he could depend on to take care of Harry.He sighed, dreading the next few hours, but turned on the spot, apparating away.Severus apparated to where he usually did  right in front of the Malfoy manner. He waved wormtail away as he opened the front gate for Snape, looking as much a rat as his animagus form. He saw no one else arriving. Severus hoped he was not the last oneto arrive at this meeting.Severus swept through the doors and into the main foyer with purpose. If anything, he had to command power and confidence when he walked among these people. It was the only way to hold some ground among the frustrating, ego-filled death eaters. He wasabout to feign boredom and indifference as usual, when the sight in front of him almost broke his resolve.He now knew why Remus had not responded to Minerva's patronus.All the death eaters were gathered in their accustomed circle  each person claiming their spot within the circle. Voldemort stood at the head of the circle as always. But this time, there was someone. In the middle of the circle, hands bound behind hisback, wand stripped from him, was Remus Lupin.It looked like he had struggled, as he saw cuts across Remus' face. His eyes were closed, and if Severus hadn't seen his chest barely moving as he breathed, he would have thought he was dead. It was all Severus had to keep his expression composed, decidingfor a look of agitation."Severus. How wonderful of you to join us," Voldemort said, his voice always just above a whisper. Severus could always see Salazar's ancestry in him. At this moment, his voice, laced with a sadistic joy, burned into Severus as he spoke. "I'm sure yourecognize our new friend who has joined us this evening."At that moment, Severus saw Remus' eyes slowly flutter open. They widened as they fell on Severus, but Remus did not move.Voldemort noticed as well. "Awake are you? Good, now we're all present." Voldemort turned towards the circle. He stepped out of his own place and paced around the circle, as was his nature."As many of you can tell, we have a guest with us today. A well done job to Fenrir, as he was able to  persuade our guest to join us this evening." Severus looked at Fenrir, as he glanced around at the group with look of pride. "He was found persuadingthe werewolves to join him and the Order, with Dumbledore." Voldemort gave a smile, one that looked more like a sick grimace. "So we thought he should be present for our meeting." Voldemort paced around the circle for 20 seconds, the silence becomingdeafening, except for the sound of his footsteps on the stone floor."Severus."Severus jerked his head up as he heard his name. Voldemort had reached back to his spot in the circle, and when he met Voldemort's eyes, Voldemort motioned to him with his wand to come forward. Severus took two steps forward, outside of the circle, towardsthe center, no expression on his face."I'm sure you two are well acquainted with eachother," Voldemort said casually, as he flicked his wand, raising Remus into the air. "Passing by eachother in the halls of Hogwarts, and through - " Voldemort laughed, "  'Order meetings'. " He raised Remusuntil his feet were no longer touching the floor. Remus struggled slightly against his bindings, but he had no energy in him."Severus, show our friend here what happens to people whoare against us." Voldemort paused, looking straight into Severus eyes. "Torture him."Severus stood still for a moment. Voldemort was staring at him intently. Severus glanced around the circle quickly. He noticed particularly, Lucius Malfoy looking at him. Watching him. He felt Lucius' stare boring into him. Waiting for what he would do.He stepped forward, taking his wand out of his robes. He slowly raised it in front of him, still expressionless. Severus looked up at the floating figure that was Remus' limp body. Remus' eyes were barely open, and his eyes came down to look at Severus.In a weak his voice, he barely made out one phrase."Severusplease."Severus' face hardened. He raised his wand as he cried out."Crucio!"A loud scream echoed through out the hollow room as Severus' spell hit. Lupin's body curled in on itself in pain, his hands still bound behind him. Lupin barely had time to breathe before Severus cast the curse on him again, and again, and again.Lucius watched as Severus continued to torture him. Lucius had been waiting for a moment like this  a moment for Severus to truly be tested. A chance to see where Severus' loyalties truly lay. He was shocked to see a glimmer of a smirk on Severus' faceas he cast spell after spell.After the seventh time of casting the curse, Remus now lay on the cold ground, unconscious. Snape put his wand down and looked up towards Voldemort, who's expression did not hide his glee."You never fail to disappoint, Severus," Voldemort said. "Let this be a warning to anyone who dares to defy the Dark Lord!" Voldemort took his wand out of his own robes. "Now, for the final touch""No."Everyone looked up towards Severus, a few light gasps around the group, as Voldemort turned towards Severus, an undecipherable expression on his face. "What did you say?"Lucius was overjoyed. His suspicions.were they right after all?Severus looked Voldemort straight in the eye. "He's no good to us dead right would be better to throw him in the Great Lake, right by Hogwarts. He will not survive the trip there in his state, anyways. And," a smirk played on Severus' lips,"it will be a good warning to the rest of them, when they see their fellow Order member  and friend  dead."Lucius was not the only one who was looking with a kind of wonder-filled shock at Severus. A smile formed on Voldemort's lips. "What an excellent idea. Lucius, Dolohov  transfer him to the Great Lake outside of Hogwarts. As for the rest of you," he turnedtowards the rest of the Death Eaters, "this particularly meeting is over for now."As the other Death Eaters stood around speaking for a moment before they dispersed, Severus swiftly walked away from the group. Lucius watched him leave, a scowl on his face.Severus walked right passed Wormtail, who was still waiting at the gates, flinging them wide open as he walked further away from Malfoy manor than he usually did. Once he was outside of site from the manor, he quickly sent two patronuses out. Then, inthe darkness of the chilly night, he disapparated away.But Severus was not going back home.Harry has never had an easy time sleeping. This night was no different. He was tossing and turning, speaking in his sleep, sweat across his brow.Suddenly, he was jolted awake, his covers thrown right off his bed. Harry was breathing hard, an indescribable terror running through his veins, tears threatening to fall from his eyes."Severus ... where are you?"
